Commands to be executed by the M\+A\+V. They can be executed on user request, or as part of a mission script. If the action is used in a mission, the parameter mapping to the waypoint/mission message is as follows\+: Param 1, Param 2, Param 3, Param 4, X\+: Param 5, Y\+:Param 6, Z\+:Param 7. This command list is similar what A\+R\+I\+N\+C 424 is for commercial aircraft\+: A data format how to interpret waypoint/mission data.

Data stream I\+Ds. A data stream is not a fixed set of messages, but rather a recommendation to the autopilot software. Individual autopilots may or may not obey the recommended messages.

These values encode the bit positions of the decode position. These values can be used to read the value of a flag bit by combining the base\+\_\+mode variable with A\+N\+D with the flag position value. The result will be either 0 or 1, depending on if the flag is set or not.
